I am just now getting back into affiliate promotions - and this is my top platform to create content other than Amazon.  It's easy to navigate, understand, and connect.</p><p class="formatted-text">Maybe the only thing, would be an easier way of logging in when I find a brand's affiliate application link - and I'm brought to the Impact join/login.  If I could pick which account number I want as I log in/apply - that would be great. Otherwise, I'm left applying with the last account number I was viewing before applying. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5000332 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering impact.com/performance:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Use it! href="https://www.g2.com/products/impact-com-performance/reviews/impact-com-performance-review-4966262"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Product enhancements galore!"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">My favorite thing about using Impact is that it's constantly evolving its product capabilities, rolling out extremely useful features for advertisers at uncommon velocity for a company of its size. The ability to discover, sort, group and transact with new partners is already miles ahead of the competition, but they keep improving it month after month. I'm also super impressed with the reporting capabilities available out of the box. Plus I've noticed the stability and access to these reports seems to get better over time. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I wouldn't say there are any downsides, but I do wish they would develop smart integrations with 3rd party CRM/Marketing tools (Hubspot, FreshSales, SFDC)  to facilitate recruitment and email campaigns at scale. Their existing newsletter messaging tool is lacking. It's barely usable. If Impact could smooth out this experience, there would be no stopping them. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4966262 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering impact.com/performance:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">In order to get the most out of the platform you need an Affiliate/Partnership marketing expert at the helm. The platform is very intuitive but the learning curve can be very steep for anyone that is new to partnership or affiliate marketing. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4966262 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Ensuring that my retail clients are working with the highest quality partners possible and providing me with the marketing intelligence to optimize those relationships. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized Impact is my favorite affilate tool to use as a marketer recommending products to my audience because they do so much right and make my job of connecting products to the right person easier. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I wish I could customize the main dashboard to quickly show what brands have converted what products. This removes a click for my audience that would otherwise reduce conversion rates.</p><p class="formatted-text"></p><p class="formatted-text">I really like the ability to track multiple brands on a single dashboard. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click </p><p class="formatted-text">They actually introduced me to brands I didn't even know they have an affiliate program.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">Smooth payments processing and great reporting  structure.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">One of the best features is contacting directly the person incharge of the affiliate program  I am interested in <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">There is nothing that I dislike, and I didn't have any issue yet with them. Other companies offer product catalogs but not always an effective way to use them. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Nothing stands out, but perhaps an easier way to glance at real-time reporting of actions from that day. Don't really need it but would be a nice feature to have. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4997985 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I'm helping people find hard-to-find items from stores they trust at a price that's fair. Sometimes that means acting quickly, but the quick link-building tools and the APIs make that possible to be effective. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle"
